149b3(mdo sde): ngan song gzhan gyi sdug bsngal las kyang thar par bgyi ba mchis sam/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rgyud gzhan dang thabs gzhan gyis gdon du rung ba yod de/ sems can gang rgyal
149b4(mdo sde): thabs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba'i rgyal por zhugs la/ longs spyod rnam pa sna tshogs la spyod pa/ chos kyi bzod pa yang mthob/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam dang yong mi ldan yang / dad pa'i mthu dang ldan
149b5(mdo sde): te/ dkon mchog gsum la rim gro dang bsti stang byed cing / sangs rgyas kyis bstan pa'i theg pa gsum dang ldan pa'i dam pa'i chos la chung ngu na tshigs su bcad pa gcig la yang 'phya zhing skur ba
149b6(mdo sde): 'ab bar du garjod pa 'am/ bgegs mi byed la/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la rab tu byung ba'i lce gnas tshul khrims can nam/ tshul khrims nyams pa 'am/ tshul khrims med kyang rung / sgra dpa
149b7(mdo sde): nas/ gos ngur smrig gyon pa thams cad la 'tshe ba dang / gnod pa dang / gzhu ba dang / 'tshig pa dang / chad pas gcod pa dang / ches gos dang / lhung bzed dang / 'tsho ba'i yo byad 'brog pa dang / chos go/
150a1(mdo sde): phrogs te khyim par phab nas/ las byed du bcug pa dang / btson rar bcug nas 'tsho ba'i dbang po dang / phral ba'i bar du mi byed la/ mchod rten dang dge 'dun gyi nor mi 'phrog pa/
150a2(mdo sde): dang / dran pa sdig pa can dag rab tu byung ba la 'tshe ba dang gnod pa byed du mi 'dzud pa dang / dkon mchog gsum gyi nor la 'phrog cing spyod du mi 'dzud pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa theg pa gsum dang /
150a3(mdo sde): ldan pa'i dam pa'i chos la bsti stang dang bcas pas mnyan cing gzungs su 'dzin pa dang / mnyan te gzungs su bzung nas kyang / ji ltar bshad pa bzhin du chos kyi rjes su brtson 'grus dang narA tan
150a4(mdo sde): byed pa dang / ngas bstan pa theg pa gsum gyi 'phags pa'i nye gnas dag la mchod pa dang / bsnyen bkur dang / bsti stang du bcas pas g.yog byed pa dang / theg pa chen po la shin tu brtan pa'i yi
150a5(mdo sde): dam bcas te/ the tshom dang / phyir ldog pa'i sems mi bskyed pa dang / gzhan yang sems can dag theg pa chen po la dad cing yid ches pa dang / gzungs su 'dzin pa dang / slob pa nan tan byed du 'jug
150a6(mdo sde): na/ rgyal rigs gdol pa can 'di dang / gzhan yang bdag nyid che ba'i gdol pa can dag ni/ snga ma 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyis kyang rgyal thabs kyi dbang bskur zhing longs spyod rnam pa sna tshogs
150a7(mdo sde): la spyod du gnang ngo // gzhan yang grong dang / grong khyer dang / nor dbyigs thams cad la spyod kyang mtshams med pa'i sems can dmyal bar mi ltung ba nas/ ngan song gzhan gyi bar du yang ltung bar mi
150b1(mdo sde): 'gyur ro// de ni ngas rgyal thabs kyi dbang bskur zhing longs spyod rnam pa sna tshogs spyod du gnang ngo // de ltar grong dang grong khyer la spyod kyang mtshams med pa'i sems can dmyal bar mi ltung ba na//
150b2(mdo sde): ngan song gzhan du yang mi ltung ngo // sems can gang sdig pa'i las kyi sgrib pa thams cad lhag ma ma lus par byang bar 'dod na/ ngas bstan pa'i dam pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la nan tan du bsra
150b3(mdo sde): cing gzungs su gzung bar bya'o// gang gis de ltar dge 'dun gyi mngon sum du gyur pa la shin tu 'dzem pa dang ngo tsha ba'i sems kyis sdig pa'i las so sor bshags na/ sngon gyi dus na
150b4(mdo sde): byas pa'i sdig pa'i las thams cad lhag ma ma lus pa dang / yongs su byang bar 'gyur ro// / 'phags pa byang chub sems dpa' sa'i snying po'i 'khor/
150b5(mdo sde): lo bcu pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo bam po brgyad pa/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje snying pos yang / bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces
150b6(mdo sde): gsol to// btsun pa bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ji ltar na nyan thos kyi theg pa lnga 'khrul pa ma mchis pa lags/ ji ltar na nyan thos kyi theg pa'i gang
150b7(mdo sde): zag la 'khrul pa ma mchis pa lags/ ji ltar na rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa ma mchis pa lags/ ji ltar na rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa ma mchis pa
151a1(mdo sde): lags/ ji ltar na theg pa chen po la 'khrul pa ma mchis pa lags/ ji ltar na theg pa chen po'i gang zag la 'khrul pa ma mchis pa lags/ ji ltar na dkon mchog
151a2(mdo sde): gsum gyi gdung rtag par yongs su 'phel bar bgyid pa lags/ ji ltar na de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la rab tu byung ba chos kyi snod dam/ chos kyi snod ma lags pa yang rung / chung ngu na chos gos kyi
151a3(mdo sde): tshal bu 'tshal zhing / skra dang kha spu bregs pa thams cad la 'khrul pa ma mchis pa lags/ ji ltar na theg pa chen po'i chos la gong nas gong du 'phar zhing phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ba lags
151a4(mdo sde): ji ltar na rno ba'i shes rab dang / bsod nams kyi khyad par rtag tu skye zhing 'phel bar 'gyur ba lags/ ji ltar na ting nge 'dzin dang / gzungs dang / bzod pa dang / sa rnams la dbang du 'gyur/
151a5(mdo sde): zhing / phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ba lags/ ji ltar na rtag tu dge bo'i bshes gnyen dang mjal cing rjes su 'thun par 'gyur ba lags/ ji ltar na rtag tu sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang /
151a6(mdo sde): mi 'bral zhing / byang chub sems dpa' dang nyan thos kyi nye gnas dang mi 'bral ba dang / chos thos pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge 'dun la mchod pa dang bsnyen bkur bgyid pa dang mi 'bral
151a7(mdo sde): bar 'gyur ba lags/ ji ltar na dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad la rab tu brtson pas sems mi ngoms pa lags/ ji ltar na byang chub kyi spyod pa rnam pa sna tshogs la sems mi ngoms pa lag/
151b1(mdo sde): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje snying po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa/
151b2(mdo sde): chen po'i 'khor lo rnam pa bcu yod de/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang 'khor lo bcu po 'di dang ldan na/ nyan thos kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// nyan thos
151b3(mdo sde): theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par gyur ro// rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// thug pa
151b4(mdo sde): chen po la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// theg pa chen po'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung rtag par yongs su 'phel bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin
151b5(mdo sde): gshegs pa'i bstan pa la rab tu byung ba chos kyi snod dam chos kyi snod ma yin pa yang rung / chung ngu na chos gos kyi tshal bu gyon cing / skra dang kha spu bregs pa thams cad la 'khrul pa med pa
151b6(mdo sde): thob par 'gyur ro// theg pa chen po'i chos la gong nas gong du 'bar zhing phyir mi ldog pa dang / rno ba'i shes rab dang / bsod nams kyi khyad par rtag tu skye zhing 'phel ba dang / ting nge 'dzin thams cad
151b7(mdo sde): dang / gzungs dang / bzod pa dang / sa rnams la dbang du 'gyur zhing / phyir mi ldog pa dang / rtag tu dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang 'phrad cing / de'i rjes su 'gro ba dang / rtag tu sangs rgyas thams cad
152a1(mdo sde): mthong ba dang mi 'bral zhing / byang chub sems dpa' dang rang sangs rgyas kyi nye gnas mthong ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / chos thos pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge 'dun la mchod//
152a2(mdo sde): pa dang bsnyen bkur byed pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad la brtson pas sems mi ngoms pa dang / byang chub kyi spyod pa dang / smon lam rnam pa sna tshogs kyi sems mi ngoms pa dang //
152a3(mdo sde): sngon sdig pa mi dge ba'i las ci byas pa thams cad 'phags pa'i chos kyi ye shes rdo rje ltar sra la rno bas lhag ma ma lus par bcom ste/ rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu mi myong ba dang / gsar du sdig
152a4(mdo sde): pa mi dge ba'i las thams cad mi byed pa dang / skyo ba dang / sgyid lug pa med pa'i sems kyis bla na med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / byang chub kyi yan lag rin po che sna bdun nan tan byed pa la skye/
152a5(mdo sde): zhing sgyid lug pa med pa'i sems dang / sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i nad rnams 'jil ba la skyo zhing sgyid lug pa med pa'i sems kyis sems can thams cad kyi rten dang gnas su 'gyur
152a6(mdo sde): zhing nye bar 'tsho ba yin no// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po rin po che sna bdun dang ldan pa ni/ gar 'gro yang rin po che'i 'khor lo thog mar 'gro ste/ rin po che gzhan de'i phyi bzhin du
152a7(mdo sde): 'brang ngo // gling bzhi kun tu rgyu zhing / sems can thams cad kyi lus dang sems kyi rnyog pa thams cad kyang bsal te/ sems can thams cad kyi lus dang sems kyi bde ba yang skye zhing 'phel bar byed do//
152b1(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pa yang de bzhin du 'khor lo bcu po 'di dang ldan na/ nyan thos kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med pa nas/ sems can thams cad kyi chen dang gnas su 'gyur ni
152b2(mdo sde): bar 'tsho ba'i bar du 'thob par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ shing rta chen po ni 'khor lo bzhi dang ldan te/ mi mang po'i nang du 'dul nas lam chen por 'gro'o// lam de na bong ba 'am/ gyo mo 'am
152b3(mdo sde): gseg ma 'am/ rtse 'am/ shing ngam/ lo ma 'am/ yal ga 'am/ me tog gam/ 'bras bu ji snyed yod pa thams cad shing na dro'i 'khor lo'i 'og tu song na/ thams cad chag cing grugs te/ nor du/
152b4(mdo sde): marung bar byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang 'khor lo rnam pa bcu dang ldan na/ nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / sems kyi sgrib pa dang / chos kyi sgrib pa thams cad
152b5(mdo sde): su com ste/ rnam par smin pa mi len par byed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ 'khor lo rnon po ni thang cig 'phangs pas pas rgol ba'i dgra'i mgo dang yan lag bcad de/ de spyod pa'i mthu med par bya
152b6(mdo sde): de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang 'khor lo rnam pa bcu po 'di dang ldan na/ rgyud lngar 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal chen po thams cad 'jims pa dang / nyon mongs pa dang / sdig
152b7(mdo sde): pa'i las thams cad yongs su bcad de rnam par smin pa len par mi byed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ ma'i bskal pa byung ba'i tshe/ nyi ma lnga cig char shar nas/ gling bzhi'i klung dang / mtsho dang / chu bo dang
153a1(mdo sde): chu'i khams su gtogs pa gsher ba thams cad gang yang mi skems pa med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang 'khor lo rnam pa bcu po 'di dang
153a2(mdo sde): ldan nA/ rgyu ba bzhi dang / nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / sems kyi sgrib pa dang / chos kyi sgrib pa dang / sdug bsngal gyi rtsa bar smin pa thams cad yongs su skems par byed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/
153a3(mdo sde): rlung gi bskal pa byung ba'i tshe/ phyogs bzhi nas rlung chen po dus gcig tu langs pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na ri bo che chung dang / sa chen po rnams thams cad 'jig cing 'thor bar 'gyur ro//
153a4(mdo sde): de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang 'khor lo rnam pa bcu dang ldan na/ 'jig rten gyi phyin ci log bzhi dang / nga rgyal gyi ri thams cad mi shigs pa gang yang med pa dang /
153a5(mdo sde): sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / sems kyi sgrib pa dang / chos kyi sgrib pa dang / sdug bsngal gyi rnam par smin pa'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang 'jig cing 'thor bar 'gyur ro// rigs
153a6(mdo sde): kyi bu 'di lta ste/ seng ge'i rgyal po ral pa can gyi skad thang gcig phyung ba'i gcan gzan thams cad 'phung ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad skrag cing 'gul mi nus par 'gyur ro// de bzhin du byang chub sems
153a7(mdo sde): dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang 'khor lo rnam pa 'di bcu dang ldan pa'i chos kyi sgra thang cig bsgrags pas mu stegs can dang / log par ston pa'i sdig pa'i grogs su gyur pa thams cad 'jigs
153b1(mdo sde): rlug nas/ smra ba'i tshig 'khrul zhing 'grib pa dang / rgol mi nus par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ brgya byin lha'i dbang po snga ma yin dang 'thab pa'i tshe/ sgra'i dmag la ga gis bskor cing
153b2(mdo sde): nirdo rdzogs te g.yul du tshugs na/ lA ma yin thams cad sreg pas ldog par 'gyur ro// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang 'khor lho rnam pa 'dri bcu dang ldan na
153b3(mdo sde): mig par lta ba'i mu stegs can thams cad dang / log par ston pa sdig pa'i grogs po thams cad sgrog nas 'bros par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che rgyas
153b4(mdo sde): mtshan gyi rtse mo la btags na/ rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs char bzhin du 'bab ste/ dbul 'phongs pa'i sems can thams cad la sbyin pa byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems
153b5(mdo sde): dpa' rnon po yang 'khor lo rnam pa 'di bcu dang ldan te/ rnam par dag pa'i tshul khrims kyi rgyal mtshan la gnas na/ chos chen po'i tshor rab tu 'bebs pas sems can tshad med pa thams
153b6(mdo sde): cad la sbyin pa byed par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ mtshan mo'i dus su 'jig rten kun mun par gyur nas 'brom zhing 'brog bslad pa na/ zla ba nya ba shar bas mun pa thams cad gsal
153b7(mdo sde): te/ 'brog bslad pa rnams kyi lam mtshon par 'gyur ba de bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang 'khor lo rnam pa 'di bcu dang ldan na/ sems can gang ma rig pa'i mun
154a1(mdo sde): pa'i mun pas madrongs te/ 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad stor ba rnams la/ byang chub sems dpa' dam pa'i chos bshad de/ ma rig pa'i mun pa thams
154a2(mdo sde): cad bsal nas/ chos kyi snang ba skyes pa'i phyir/ 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad mngon du gyur te/ zag pa thams cad zad nas sdug bsngal gyi mtha' zad par byed do// rigs kyi bu/
154a3(mdo sde): 'di lta ste/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'jig rten du shar ba dang / lo tog thams cad skye zhing 'phel te/ me tog dang / lo tog dang lo ma thams cad rgyas pa dang / mnam
154a4(mdo sde): zhing btsog pa thams cad sel ba dang / lo tog gri 'bru dang / sman gyi 'bras bu thams cad smin pa dang / gangs kyi ri bo zhu bas 'bab chu kun brug ste/ rim gyis rgya mtsho chen por 'bab par
154a5(mdo sde): 'gyur ro// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang 'khor lo rnam pa 'di bcu dang ldan te/ lhag pa'i sbyin pa la gnas shing dul ba'i tshul khrims dang / bde ba'i bzod
154a6(mdo sde): pa dang / brtson 'grus dang / bsam gtan dang / shes rab dang / thabs dang / byams pa dang / snying rje dang / spobs pa'i yon tan shin tu rgyas shing / sems can thams cad la dam pa'i
154a7(mdo sde): chos ston to// chos de'i 'od kyi gzi brjid kyi sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba lhag pa'i lo tog rnam pa sna tshogs skye zhing 'phel ba dang / lhag pa'i spyod pa dam pa'i me tog dang / lo/
154b1(mdo sde): ma rnam pa sna tshogs shin tu rgyus pa dang / nyon mongs pa'i las ngan pa thams cad yongs su sel ba dang / mtho ris dang mya ngan las 'da' ba'i 'bras bu yongs su smin par 'gyur ba dang /
154b2(mdo sde): log par lte ba dang / nga rgyal gyi ri bo thams cad zhu zhing 'bab pas yang dag pa'i dad pa dang / tshul khrims dang / thos pa dang / gtong ba dang / shes rab dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi chu rim gyis/
154b3(mdo sde): 'bab cing / mya ngan las 'da' ba'i rgya mtsho 'gengs pa dang / sems can thams cad yid bzhin du 'jigs pa med pa mya ngan las 'da' ba'i grong khyer du 'jug par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu de
154b4(mdo sde): la ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i 'khor lo bcu gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'khor lo bcu zhes bya ba ni/ chos gzhan la mi gdags kyi/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam nyid
154b5(mdo sde): yin par shes par bya'o// 'khor lo rnam pa bcu po 'di dag dag dang ldan pas na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zhes bya ste/ sdig pa thams cad las rnam par grol ba dang /
154b6(mdo sde): dge ba'i chos thams cad yid bzhin du rdzogs pa dang / myur du mya ngan las 'da' ba'i chen po'i rgya mtsho yongs su 'gengs pa dang / thabs mkhas pa chen po'i ye shes kyi 'od kyis skye
154b7(mdo sde): bo thams cad yongs su smin par byed cing / thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba yongs su thob par byed do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu snga ma 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
155a1(mdo sde): thams cad kyis kyang mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam yongs su spangs te/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'di la yongs su bsngags pas 'bras bu thob par gyur to// de bas na/
155a2(mdo sde): gang gis dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'di dag las 'ga' zhig na ma 'tsho ba'i bar du ma nyams par srung na/ 'bras bu khyad par can mchog tu 'gyur ba thams cad thob pa ni ji ltar bshad pa bzhin no//
155a3(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang nam 'tsho ba'i bar du srog gcod pa yongs su spangs na/ de nyid sems can thams cad la mi 'jigs pa sbyin pa yin te/
155a4(mdo sde): sems can dag la 'jigs shing bag tsha bar mi byed pas/ de'i 'jigs pa'i sdug bsngal mi bskyed pa'i dbang gis/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad myur du yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// thog ma
155a5(mdo sde): med pa'i mtha' nas rgyud lngar 'khor ba'i rgya mtshor bying ba/ srog gcod pa'i dbang gis telus dang / ngag dang / yid kyi sdig pa mi dge ba'i las bdag kyang byed la/ gzhan yang byed du 'jug cing/
155a6(mdo sde): mthong ba dang thos pa'i rjes su yi rang ba las byung ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / sems kyi sgrib pa dang / chos kyi sgrib pa dang / tshe'i sgrib pas bsgribs par gyur to// 'di ltar srog gcod pa/
155a7(mdo sde): yongs su spangs pa'i las de dag lhag ma ma lus par yongs su bcom zhing brnyil bas rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu mi myong bar byed do// lus 'di nyid la yang lha dang mi sogs pa kun dga' zhing //
155b1(mdo sde): yid du 'ong ba dang / dogs pa mi skye ba dang / lus drang sems rab tu bde zhing yun ring du 'tsho bar 'gyur ro// 'chi 'pho ba'i dus byed pa na yang lus dang sems la sdug bsngal gyis mi gdung zhing yid du/
155b2(mdo sde): 'ong ba'i bu dang / chung ma dang / 'khor thams cad kyis yongs su bskor bas 'chi 'pho bo'i dus byed kyi/ shin tu 'jigs pa'i gshin rje'i po nya mthong bar mi 'gyur ro// gnan yang srid du 'ong ba'i
155b3(mdo sde): dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos kyis dul ba/ tshul khrims drang yon tan du ldan pa/ bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa dang 'phrad de/ lus dang sems rab tu dga' ba dang / de la bkur sti dang bcas
155b4(mdo sde): par shin tu dad pa skye bar 'gyur ro// yang tshe 'phos nas kyang phyir mi'i nang du skyes te/ dbang po yongs su rdzogs shing yan lag dang ldan pa dang / gang nas gang du skyes par nad med pa dang / tshe ring ba
155b5(mdo sde): dang / byung gzugs bzang ba dang / yid gzhungs pa dang / rab tu bde zhing spyod pa dang / gzhan yid du 'ong ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos kyis dul ba/ tshul khrims dang yon tan du ldan pa/ bsod
155b6(mdo sde): rnams kyi zhing yang dag pa dang zad de/ de'i rjes su srab pa dang / srog gcod pa yongs su spang ba dang / sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos thams cad yongs su gcod pa dang / dge ba'i chos byed par
155b7(mdo sde): cad yongs su rdzogs pa dang / theg pa chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs thams cad tshol ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sngon lam dang / spyod pa thams cad la rim gyis gnol zhing / shin tu yangs
156a1(mdo sde): pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho la 'jug pa nas/ bla na med pa'i byang chub thob pa'i bar tu 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtshon cha med pa dang / dgra dang 'tshe ba'i ming mi grag pa
156a2(mdo sde): dang / 'jigs pa thams cad dang bral te/ rab tu bde zhing skyed pa dang / nad med pa dang / tshe ring ba'i zhing du sems can dag skye bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshe'i tshad kyang dpag tu med de/
156a3(mdo sde): sems can dag cis 'dul ba bzhin du dam pa'i chos ston to// yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas kyang / dam pa'i chos yun ring du gnas shing sems can tshad med pa la phan pa dang bde ba'i don
156a4(mdo sde): byed par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po srog gcod pa yongs su spangs pa'i 'khor lo ste dang po'o// // byang chub sems dpa'
156a5(mdo sde): sems dpa' chen po 'khor lo de dang ldan na/ nyan thos kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ nyan thos kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// rang sangs rgyas kyis theg pa/
156a6(mdo sde): la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// theg pa chen po la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ theg pa chen po'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med
156a7(mdo sde): par 'gyur ro// dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung yongs su 'phel ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la rab tu byung ba'i nye gnas ros kyi snod dam chos kyi snod ma yin pa yang rung / chung ngu na
156b1(mdo sde): chos gos kyi tshal bu gyon cing / skra dang kha spu bregs pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// theg pa chen po'i chos la gong nas gong du 'phar zhing phyir mi ldog pa dang / rno ba'i shes rab dang / bsod
156b2(mdo sde): rnams kyi byung par rtag tu skye zhing 'phel ba dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / gzungs drang / brjod pa dang / sa rnams thams cad la dbang du 'gyur zhing phyir mi ldog pa dang / rtag tu dge ba'i bshes gnyen
156b3(mdo sde): dadang 'brang cing rjes su 'gro ba dang / rtag tu sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang mi 'bral zhing / byang chub sems dpa' dang / nyan thos kyi cha gnas mthong ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / chos thos pa dang mi
156b4(mdo sde): 'bral ba dang / dge 'dun la mchod pa dang bsnyen bkur byed pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad rgol ba la brtson pas sems mi ngoms pa dang / byang chub kyi spyod pa dang / smon lam rmam
156b5(mdo sde): pa sna tshogs kyi sems mi ngoms par 'gyur te/ 'bras bu gzhan thob pa yang ji ltar rgyas par bshad pa bzhin no// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang num
156b6(mdo sde): 'chi ba'i bar du ma byin par len pa yongs su spangs na/ de nyid sems can thams cad la mi 'jigs pa sbyin pa yin te/ yongs su gdung ba med pa dang / 'tshe ba med pa dang / bdag nyid tshul bzhin
156b7(mdo sde): du rung ba'i nor gyis chog shes par gnas kyi/ chos ma yin pa'i nor dang khe la re ba med pa de'i dbang gis dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// thog ma med pa'i
157a1(mdo sde): mtha' nas rgyu lngar 'khor zhing 'khor ba'i rgya mtshor bying bar 'gyur ba yang ma byin par len pa'i dbang gis lus dang / ngag dang / yid mi dge ba'i las rnams bdag/
157a2(mdo sde): kyang byed la/ gzhan yang byed du 'dzud cing / mthong ba dang thos pa'i rjes su ya~M rang ba las byung ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / sems kyi sgrib pa dang / chos kyi sgrib pa dang / rin po che dang nor/
157a3(mdo sde): lnga sgrib pas bsgrib par gyur to// 'di ltar ma byin par len pa yongs su spangs pa'i 'khor los lhag ma ma lus par yongs su bcom pas rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu mi myong ste/ lus 'di
157a4(mdo sde): nyid la'ang lha dang mi la sogs pa kun dga' zhing / yid du 'ong bas dogs pa mi skye ba dang / lus dang sems rab tu bde ba dang / nor rin po che thams cad dang ldan par 'gyur ro// nam
157a5(mdo sde): 'chi 'pho ba'i dus byed pa na yang lus dang sems la sdug bsngal gyis mi gdung zhing yid du 'ong ba'i bu dang / chung ma dang / 'khor thams cad kyis yongs su bskor bar 'chi 'phos pa'i dus byed kyi
157a6(mdo sde): shin tu 'jigs pa'i gshin rje'i pho nya mthong bar mi 'gyur ro// gzhan yid du 'ong ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos kyis dul ba/ tshul khrims dang yon tan du ldan pa/ bsod nams kyi zhing yang
157a7(mdo sde): dag pa dang phrad de/ lus dang sems rab tu dga' ba dang / de la bkur sti dang bcas pas dad pa skye bar 'gyur ro// tshe 'phos nas kyang phyir mi'i nang du skyes te/ dbang po yong su rdzogs shing yan lag
157b1(mdo sde): dang ldan pa dang / gdunas gang du skyes par longs spyod chen po dang ldam ning byang gdugs bzang ba dang / yid gzungs pa dang / rab tu 'ang zhing sring pa dang / 'jigs pa lnga dang / nor blan myong dung/
157b2(mdo sde): 'gyur ro// phyir yang yid du 'ong ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos kyis dul ba/ tshul khrims dang yon tan du ldan pa/ bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa dang phrad de/ de'i rjes su slob cing ma byin par
157b3(mdo sde): len pa yongs su spong ba dang / sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos thams cad yongs su gcod pa dang / dge ba'i chos khyad par can thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa dang / theg pa chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs
157b4(mdo sde): thams cad tshol ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam dang / spyod pa thams cad la rim gyis gnol ba dang / shin tu yangs pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho la 'jug pa nas/ bla na med pa'i byang chub kyi bar
157b5(mdo sde): du 'thob par 'gyur ro// yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa dang / rin po che'i shing dang / rin po che'i rdzing dang / rin po che'i gzhal med khang la sogs pas yongs su
157b6(mdo sde): gang ba dang / bdag dang bdag gir 'dzin pa dang bral ba/ rgyan thams cad kyis bkod pa dang ldan pa'i ning der sems can bdag skye bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshe'i tshad kyang dngag tu
157b7(mdo sde): med de/ sems can dag cis 'dul ba bzhin du dam pa'i chos ston to// yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas kyang / dam pa'i chos yun ring du gnas shing / sems can tshad med pa la phan pa dang bde
158a1(mdo sde): ba'i don byed par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos ma byin par len pa yongs su spangs pa'i 'khor lo gnyis pa'o//
158a2(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'khor lo 'di dang ldan ni/ nyan thos kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ nyan thos kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// rang
158a3(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// theg pa chen po la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ theg pa chen po'i gang zag la/

158b3(mdo sde): chen po gang nam 'tsha ba'i bar du 'ding bas log par g.yem pa yongs su spangs na/ de nyid sems can thams cad 'dod pa'i klung gis g.yengs pa lngas 'jigs pa med pag/ phrag dog med pa/
158b4(mdo sde): ba med pa/ yongs su gdung ba med pa/ 'khrug pa med pa'i sbyin pa yin te/ bdag gi chung ma'i chog shes shing / gzhan gyi chung ma wa ra ba med pas/ de'i dbang gis dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su
158b5(mdo sde): rdzogs par 'gyur ro// thog ma med pa'i mtha' nas rgyud lngar 'khor bar 'khor ba'i rgya mtshor 'bying ba yang 'dod pas logs par g.yem pa'i dbang grisA lus dang / ngag dang / yid mi dge ba'i las

175b1(mdo sde): dang ye shes 'thob// rtag tu bden pa smra bar dgal// brdzun du 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal 'jil// tshig gcig tshang mar btsugs pas ma// sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun mthong // brdzun mi smra
175b2(mdo sde): bla bsgoms pas ma// byang chub chen po myur du 'thob// phra ma'i tshig sgra yongs spangs na// dge ba'i chos kyi snod du 'gyur// sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun mthong // chad par lta bar yongs
175b3(mdo sde): mi 'gyur// 'phags pa'i chags med dga' ba dang // rin chen gter gyi gzungs 'thob cing // zab mo'i chos kyi rgya mtsho rig/ myur du bla med byang chub 'thob// gal te zhe gcod tshig spa
175b4(mdo sde): te// 'jam zhing gnyen pa'i tshig smras na// sems can kun gyis bkur bar 'gyur// snga ma'i mi dge'i las kyang zhi// 'khor rnams rtag tu dga' ba dang // byang chub sems dpa'i ston
175b5(mdo sde): par 'gyur// sangs rgyas mang po'i spyod yul shes// sa bcu las kyang 'da' bar 'gyur// bkyil par smra ba yongs spangs na// mkhas par bkur zhing bla ma byed// gzhan la tshig tu smra
175b6(mdo sde): ba kun// yon tan rnam lnga 'thob par 'gyur// rtag tu 'phags pa'i tshig nyan cing // 'phags pa'i lam tshul spro bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas rgya mtsho yongs rdzogs shing // thams cad
175b7(mdo sde): mkhyen pa myur du 'thob// gal te chags sems yongs spangs te/ 'phags pa rnams la mi spod cing // ngur smrig gyon la mchod pa byed// theg pa gsum gyi byang chub bsgrub// rtag tu rnam/
176a1(mdo sde): ngag zhing du skye// ston pa'i gnas su gnas par 'gyur// bla med theg pa la zhon te// rgyal ba'i ye shes myur du 'thob// gal te gnod sems yongs spangs te/
176a2(mdo sde): gcig tu byams pa'i sems bsgoms na/ mnyam par bzhag pa'ang myur du 'thob// 'phags pa'i spyod yul mos par 'gyur// rnam dag sangs rgyas zhing du skye// nyes pa'i skyon rnams
176a3(mdo sde): kun dang bral// de la gnas na byang chub 'thob// gnod sems thams cad spong bar bya// ngan par lta ba yongs spangs te// rnam dag dad pa'i sems bsgoms na// theg gsum ston la mos
176a4(mdo sde): byed cing // sangs rgyas kun la mchod pa byed// ngan song kun las yongs thar te// 'phags pa'i dge 'dun rnams dang phrad// byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan ldan// ye shes mchog
176a5(mdo sde): kyang 'thob par 'gyur// dge ba bcu yi las lam gyis// byang chub mchog 'thob 'gyur zhes gsungs// snyoms par 'jug dang gzungs rnams dang // sa dang bzod pa skye bar 'gyur//
176a6(mdo sde): dgra nyid che ba'i 'khor lo 'dis// ngan song thams cad rab bcom nas// sdig pa'i sgrib pa kun kyang choms// myur du byang chub chen po 'thob// 'phags pa shin tu rgyas pa chen po
176a7(mdo sde): sa'i snying po'i 'khor lo bcu pa zhes bya ba las// dge ba'i las kyi lam zhes bya ba'i le'u ste drug go// / rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems
176b1(mdo sde): dpa' chen po zang zing gi sbyin pa'i go cha chen po'i 'khor lo rnam pa bcu yod do// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang 'khor lo de dag dang ldan na// thog ma sems bskyed/
176b2(mdo sde): pa nas/ 'dod pa lnga yongs su bsal te/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad las shin tu 'das nas/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing chen por
176b3(mdo sde): 'gyur ba dang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa thams cad kyis mchod pa dang / srung ba dang / bsnyen bkur byed par 'gyur ro// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ rnam pa sna tshogs kyi
176b4(mdo sde): zas dang / snyoms dang / gos dang / rin po che'i brgyan dang / ba glang dang / rta dang / shing rta dang / lus kyi yan lag dang / rkang pa dang / lag pa dang / rna ba dang / sna dang / mgau dang / mig
176b5(mdo sde): dang / rkang dang / klad pa dang / pags pa dang / rus pa dang / sha dang / khrag dang / yul dang / srid dang / bu dang / chung ma dang / bran+da po dang / bran mo dang / khang khyim dang / zhing 'brog la sogs
176b6(mdo sde): pa de dag thams cad sbyin pa de re re byed na/ lus dang srog la mi lta zhing / bdag gcig pu 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bde ba 'dod pa'i phyir sems bskyed de sbyin pa byed pa ma
176b7(mdo sde): yin gyi/ sems can thams cad la byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen po'i myur gu bskyed pa'i phyir sbyin pa sbyin pa'i sems skyed do// thabs mkhas pa dang / shes rab mchog skyed pa'i phyir skye
177a1(mdo sde): pa sbyin pa'i sems
